\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ridge_8py_source_l00153}00153\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{\#\ Add\ penalty\ alpha\ *\ ||coef||\_2\string^2\ for\ alpha=1\ and\ solve\ via\ normal\ equations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ridge_8py_source_l00154}00154\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{\#\ Note\ that\ the\ problem\ is\ well\ conditioned\ such\ that\ we\ get\ accurate\ results.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ridge_8py_source_l00155}00155\ \ \ \ \ alpha\ =\ 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ridge_8py_source_l00156}00156\ \ \ \ \ d\ =\ alpha\ *\ np.identity(n\_features)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{test__ridge_8py_source_l00157}00157\ \ \ \ \ d[-\/1,\ -\/1]\ =\ 0\ \ \textcolor{comment}{\#\ intercept\ gets\ no\ penalty}}
